<text>Fantastic pupusas!

I plan on returning to try more of their menu, but first impression was already an outstanding one.

We tried a mixed, spinach, and chicharon. As you can see from the pictures, the sheer size made the reasonable price a bargain. Quantity of food only goes so far, but this restaurant had the quality to match! Stretchy cheese, FRESH (so fresh, probably a good idea to let them cool a bit before that first bite), and satisfying.

The mixed pupusa had a more cheese and bean prominent flavor profile, but if you want a more meat forward option, get the chicharon! More of a carnitas consistency than the crunchy, fried pork rinds most associate with the term chicharon, it is a filling and delicious option.

The spinach was less prominent, but still added to the cheese. I felt this and the mixed best paired with the repollo (slaw is the best word I can think of for translation) and sauce. With the occasional slice of jalape√±o, it made for a touch of spice and a bit more acid to a more rich flavor.

Can't wait to go back!<//text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMzoTLfeMxNBgGoWW5c2lXvaYYIkDDJo6G9fUNl=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipODbgoq8tLLpcpeqZ1m2fZAvj8WsfILCo5Cye8q=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMv1_wX3sEYWEO5DovqxgzXYBCFcHMiO_BHyTZR=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN3AtCHgNIAslqA9RSv-L8izGJ-JS0VYFm4_bS2=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN7kBXwWqCHjKuuVKYU5d6IuUvZ24Xt3zcbMEPA=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMbqlbqjGLuFQvt9bgWx0YxWY2NLPnaFWNJseG0=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMUXbhYKVDtqeIaiPBXD8O9rAELXTeqH-pO-1xo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPd9Cx9CyhtlRw3NA0pN195PaKeLSV7C-hZ1932=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOujqseIMjp67x52zKcOv8MVIVZcKjbLu1miAzo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPE7n9ycUTt3BCGbeaG_lQMHwjL1o3Kg0Ti7IYF=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNrokqjNeIFxBkvtpgWq9qVXw_-_GpujHNAIkTZ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNDbcVgHD1Py4QW56zCQEkC_BTgpyoklcDNYtjJ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures>< Resp>

< Review>
Not the best quality Mexican restaurant in San Leandro and not the cheapest. They aren't terrible or even bad, the service is usually friendly enough and the food isnt terrible but you can tell it isn't the highest quality. I would personally recommend at least three other Mexican restaurants over this one. I usually go here only for a quick bite since it is around the corner from where I live. The two star rating seems low but I would go back purely out of convenience.<//Review>

This is why you should not visit The Glass Warehouse.

1. The price you pay for products, changes by as much as 100% every day.
2. No matter how much you spend, they will never remember you or care.
3. They lie about the glass quality, and refuse to bargain on EXTREMELY overpriced products.
4. When they sell you something cheap, they will not replace it if it malfunctions, or breaks.
5. They will give you 10% off if they are feeling nice that day.
6. The wraps are always dry when they promise that they are fresh.
7. They refuse to give you the same price on coils each time you visit. Again, prices are never the same.
8. They do not always ask for ID, and then they will act like cops on a different day, making you feel uncomfortable when you walk in the door.
9. The owners are never around, so when you need to complain about being ripped off, "everyone" is the owner.
10. They are a super-sized smoke shop, and they have no need to meet your needs as another customer will walk in and pay a 300% markup without question.
11. They treat their employees like DIRT.
12. They switch out the original down-stems and bows for the cheapest ones possible, and then place them on the shelf for sale. To get your bong's original bowl that it came with, you must pay a premium price separately from the bong you are buying.

Yesterday, they sold my friend and I Kanger Mega Coils @ 5 for 10 Dollars.
Today, I tried to buy more coils, and they were priced at 4.35 each, NO BULK DISCOUNT, and NO PACKS. ONLY SINGLES. WTF? Yesterday I just bought 5 coils for $10? And overnight they jump to $4.35 a piece?

< userid>
113464365643852366593< /userid>
<name>ËÉ°Â≠êÊÅ©</name><date>1439269716294</date><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
Me and my family brought 5 of our other family members who just came visit us from Taiwan, all of us were very satisfied with the quality of the foods there. My wife said that the rice box is even better than the one we had the most in Taipei. My youngest sister said the cold noodle she ordered was surprisingly tasty. All of us ordered different kind of dishes and we all loved it. We will definitely come again when we are nearby.

The restaurant declared they put no MSG and any artificial additives into their foods, they also cook their food with purified water. Those are the ones I concern the most, and I never had such a good experience with a Taiwanese restaurant around Rowland Heights and Irvine area, where I just moved to about half a year ago. It is not too salty, not too oily, but tastes GOOD! Also the dining environment is comfortable, I would say among most of the other Chinese restaurants around RH and Irvine I had before.

Try it once and you will know how good and healthy Taiwanese foods can be.</text>

<Rating>2<//Rating>< Text>
What a disappointment!  Should have turned and left when I saw how out of place this restaurant was in a plaza occupied by Trader Joe's.  But, then again, out of place restaurants usually have the best food (at least from my experience).  Why Thirsty, however, isn't one of these places.

To start, if you can't read Chinese, don't EVEN bother showing up to this place.  It's the first Asian restaurant I've been to that have menus that's ALL in Chinese!  Thank God I went to Chinese School!

I ordered the Beef Noodle and it was MEH.  The beef wasn't that tender and the noodle/broth was fairly typical.  I tried the pork chop and it wasn't anything special either.  I've definitely experienced better.

Overall, I was disappointed.  I thought it would be pretty good since it was rated 4 stars on Yelp and there seems to be a never ending line of people wanting to get a table.  Maybe I'm missing something they're aware of?< /Text>

< text>
All my family photos were saved by BYOD from my failed hard drive from 10 years ago.  I have been saving years of photos and I finally had a chance to do some archiving work when my hard drive died.  I went to three different places in West LA and nobody could do it, or at least do it for a reasonable price... One place wanted to charge me $1500.  Anyway I just kept on looking around and while I have to drive all the way closer to downtown LA is was worth the trip.  They were so accommodating and they gave me a good deal.  It still was not cheap by any stretch of imagination but it was enough for me to make a whole sense of it all.  I gave the go signal, and after a week  they called in to tell me that all my archives were recovered.  I am so thankful to these guys at BYOD and they truly deserve all the accolades that they got!  Here's another one for the books!  Many thanks and I appreciate the great service!<//text>

My G-Drive external hard drive crashed just before finals week and I was in panic mode. All of my notes and project files were on that drive. I went on a deep dive in Google and found BYOD.

My research paid off. They recovered all my files and also did it just in time for me to study for my finals. I'm glad I found them otherwise I probably would have failed this semester! Thank you BYOD! I would definitely recommend you guys to all my classmates!< /Text>

As a result the first moving company we hired had to put all our belongings into a storage facility.  When we finally were given closing docs I called Maison Moving.

I do not recommend this company.

These individuals use a very poor tactic of bait and switch to increase the cost you have to pay at the end of the move.

I recently used this service to help move my family. When I spoke to Mellissa initially, she gave me a very fair and upfront cost for the move that made the deal enticing. After double checking all the details over serval days before the move, (I literally called almost everyday), we were all set for the service. Mellisa informed me that the time estimated for the move was going to be around 4 hours which included drive time. REMEMBER THIS, ITS IMPORTANT!  The company doubles the drive time in the estimate to allow for traffic if there is any.

The guys that showed up were professional and fairly quick at their job so I‚Äôm not faulting them for this.

Where I found the issue was the final price they tried to give me. After the move took 5 and a half hours the dispatcher then increased the time to 6 hours and 45 minutes. He then claimed that with the drive time doubled it isn‚Äôt included within the time estimate. HERES THE ISSUE. Never, not once was I informed that the price of the move was going to be the time it took for the move, then add the drive time ON TOP of the total. Again this a very poor bait and switch tactic to make the customer over pay for the services. They don‚Äôt inform you fully until after the move is done so you have little to no choice.

If you do use these services I highly recommend you work into your contract or service agreement to remove this aspect so you don‚Äôt get falsely charged for excess services. These charges are supposed to be included within the time estimation and not added on top of.

AGAIN, I can stress this enough do not use these services. They are not people who treat their customers fairly.

I have already filed a complaint with the BBB to help ensure that these people don‚Äôt overcharge any further customers.<//text>
